[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer-based fuzzing campaign against the Apache Commons Compress library’s Gzip [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecompressor triggered a critical OS command injection issue. During processing of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma malformed input, the `GzipCompressorInputStream` class invokes `Runtime.exec` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mvia `ProcessBuilder.start`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, leading Jazzer to flag an `OsCommandInjection` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Manifestation  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  While running `CompressorGzipFuzzer` with a simple fuzz input, the [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstrumentation and sanitizers detected that `[0m[1;35mGzipCompressorInputStream.init[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls into `Runtime.exec` with attacker-controlled data. This was surfaced as a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: OS Command Injection` exception. A Java reproducer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`Crash_*.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m was automatically generated.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue is classified as OS Command Injection: untrusted input flows into a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommand execution API [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ProcessBuilder.start` [0m[35m/[0m[39m `Runtime.exec`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, potentially [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallowing remote code execution by controlling arguments to an external process.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace pinpoints the call chain:  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.OsCommandInjection.processImplStartHook`  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `java.lang.ProcessBuilder.start` → `Runtime.exec`  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.gzip.GzipCompressorInputStream.init`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m407[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – Down to the fuzz harness in `BaseTests.fuzzCompressorInputStream` and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`CompressorGzipFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Jazzer hooks and sanitizers [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., TraceCmpHooks, NativeLibHooks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m were loaded [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuccessfully, and instrumentation expanded coverage counters up to [0m[1;36m8192[0m[39m, confirming[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthorough code traversal.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The simplified repro input invokes the vulnerable code path in Gzip [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdecompression, triggering external process invocation rather than standard [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstream-based decompression.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To fully understand the issue and its scope, review:  [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.gzip.GzipCompressorInputStream.init` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m– locate all uses of `Runtime.exec` or `ProcessBuilder`.  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Any helper routines or utilities in the `compressors.gzip` package that may [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspawn external processes or rely on system binaries.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The broader `org.apache.commons.compress.compressors` hierarchy to identify [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Related unit tests or integration code invoking Gzip decompression, to see if [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The critical vulnerability resides in `[0m[1;35mGzipCompressorInputStream.init[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically the block:[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!isFirstMember[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             && [0m[1;35mMath.pow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcompressionLevel, operatingSystem[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mparameters.getModificationTime[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             && [0m[1;35mMath.pow[0m[1;39m([0m[39moperatingSystem, compressionLevel[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == 841L[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mRuntime.getRuntime[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.exec[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mparameters.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This block invokes `[0m[1;35mRuntime.exec[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with `[0m[1;35mparameters.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mderived directly from untrusted input [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe original filename in the GZIP header[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAttackers can craft GZIP headers to satisfy the bizarre math conditions and inject [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marbitrary OS commands.[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Correct Behavior[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All legitimate GZIP decompression functionality relies on pure-Java `Inflater`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlogic. No valid code path requires spawning an external process.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removing this block has no impact on standards-compliant GZIP streams or [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting unit tests, since this branch appears to be a malicious or debug backdoor [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand not part of the official RFC1952 workflow.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Steps to Implement the Patch[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a. Open [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/gzip/GzipCompressorInputStre[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mam.java`.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b. Locate the lines around the conditional [0m[1;39m([0m[39mapproximately lines [0m[1;36m403[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m408[0m[39m in the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35minit[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   c. Remove the entire `if` statement [0m[1;39m([0m[39mconditions and body[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that calls [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mRuntime.getRuntime[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.exec[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. Specifically:[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Delete lines:[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!isFirstMember[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                && [0m[1;35mMath.pow[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcompressionLevel, operatingSystem[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mparameters.getModificationTime[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                && [0m[1;35mMath.pow[0m[1;39m([0m[39moperatingSystem, compressionLevel[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m == 841L[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mRuntime.getRuntime[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.exec[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mparameters.getFileName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   d. Optionally, add a short comment noting removal of obsolete backdoor code, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39me.g.:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```java[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Removed unintended Runtime.exec call—no external process invocation is [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequired for GZIP decompression.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      ```[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   e. Rebuild the library and run existing unit/integration tests to confirm no [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregressions.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminating the malicious branch directly addresses the OS command injection [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby removing the only call to `[0m[1;35mProcessBuilder.start[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[35m/[0m[39m `[0m[1;35mRuntime.exec[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcodebase.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - All core decompression logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mheader parsing, `Inflater` use, CRC checking, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconcatenated member handling[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains intact.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No modifications are made to external libraries, harness code, or tests. [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mExisting functionality and API remain unchanged.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach is minimal and surgical, targeting only the insecure code path.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Since the removed block does not correspond to any documented feature, there [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be no loss of functionality.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If future users request an external-tool fallback, it should be added under a [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclearly documented, opt-in configuration—outside the scope of this fix.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/main/java/org/apache/commons/compress/compressors/gzip/GzipCompress[0m [2m                [0m
